                // Fallback javascript, when the ad Service call fails.  
                
                if((window.csm === undefined || window.generic === undefined || window.consoleLog === undefined)) {

         <h1 class="header">
          Quotes
         </h1>
        </div>
        <div class="header" id="quotes_content">
         <div class="header">
          <div class="nav">
           <div class="desc">
            Showing all 110 items
           </div>

         <div class="list">
          <div class="quote soda sodavote odd" id="qt0371383">
           <div class="sodatext">
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000111/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Adult Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
I know what I have to do. But going back means I'll have to face my past. I've been running from it for so long.
            </p>
            <p>
             [
             <span class="fine">
              Rafiki hits Simba on the head with his stick
             </span>
             ]
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000111/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Adult Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Ow! Jeez, what was that for?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0347039/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Rafiki
              </span>
             </a>
             :
It doesn't matter. It's in the past.
            </p>
            <p>
             [
             <span class="fine">
              laughs
             </span>
             ]
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000111/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Adult Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Yeah, but it still hurts.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0347039/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Rafiki
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Oh yes, the past can hurt. But from the way I see it, you can either run from it, or... learn from it.
            </p>
            <p>
             [
             <span class="fine">
              swings his stick again at Simba, who ducks out of the way
             </span>
             ]
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0347039/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Rafiki
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Ha. You see? So what are you going to do?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000111/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Adult Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
First, I'm gonna take your stick.
            </p>
            <p>
             [
             <span class="fine">
              Simba snatches Rafiki's stick and throws it and Rafiki runs to grab it
             </span>
             ]
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0347039/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Rafiki
              </span>
             </a>
             :
No, no, no, no, not the stick! Hey, where you going?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000111/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Adult Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
I'm going back!
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0347039/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Rafiki
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Good! Go on! Get out of here!
            </p>
            <p>
             [
             <span class="fine">
              Rafiki begins laughing and screeching loudly
             </span>
             ]
            </p>

          <div class="quote soda sodavote even" id="qt0371442">
           <div class="sodatext">
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0347039/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Rafiki
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Asante sana Squash banana, Wiwi nugu Mi mi apana.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000111/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Adult Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Come on, will you cut it out?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0347039/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Rafiki
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Can't cut it out. It will grow right back. Hehehe.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000111/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Adult Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Creepy little monkey. Would you stop following me! Who are you?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0347039/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Rafiki
              </span>
             </a>
             :
The question is, who... are you?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000111/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Adult Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              sighs
             </span>
             ]
I thought I knew, but now I'm not so sure.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0347039/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Rafiki
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Well, I know who you are! Shh. Come here, it's a secret.
            </p>
            <p>
             [
             <span class="fine">
              Whispers, then grows louder
             </span>
             ]
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0347039/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Rafiki
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Asante sana Squash banana, Wiwi nugu Mi mi apana!
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000111/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Adult Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Enough already! What's that supposed to mean, anyway?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0347039/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Rafiki
              </span>
             </a>
             :
It means you're a baboon... and I'm not.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000111/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Adult Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
I think you're a little confused.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0347039/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Rafiki
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Wrong! I'm not the one who's confused. You don't even know who you are!
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000111/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Adult Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Oh, and I suppose you know?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0347039/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Rafiki
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Sure do. You're Mufasa's boy!
            </p>
            <p>
             [
             <span class="fine">
              Simba turns around to look at him, shocked
             </span>
             ]
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0347039/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Rafiki
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Bye!
            </p>
           </div>

          <div class="quote soda sodavote odd" id="qt0371375">
           <div class="sodatext">
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0754676/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Pumbaa
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Hey, Timon, ever wonder what those sparkly dots are up there?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001447/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Timon
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Pumbaa, I don't wonder; I know.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0754676/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Pumbaa
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Oh. What are they?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001447/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Timon
              </span>
             </a>
             :
They're fireflies. Fireflies that, uh... got stuck up on that big bluish-black thing.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0754676/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Pumbaa
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Oh, gee. I always thought they were balls of gas burning billions of miles away.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001447/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Timon
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Pumbaa, with you, everything's gas.
            </p>

          <div class="quote soda sodavote even" id="qt0371365">
           <div class="sodatext">
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0347039/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Rafiki
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              after guiding Simba to a spot where he says will show him Mufasa
             </span>
             ]
Look down there.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000111/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Adult Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              looks into a pool of water
             </span>
             ]
That's not my father. That's just my reflection.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0347039/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Rafiki
              </span>
             </a>
             :
No, look harder.
            </p>
            <p>
             [
             <span class="fine">
              touches the water, as it ripples Simba's reflection changes to that of his father
             </span>
             ]
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0347039/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Rafiki
              </span>
             </a>
             :
You see? He lives in you.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000469/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Mufasa's ghost
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              from above
             </span>
             ]
Simba.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000111/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Adult Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Father?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000469/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Mufasa's ghost
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              apears among the stars
             </span>
             ]
Simba, you have forgotten me.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000111/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Adult Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
No. How could I?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000469/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Mufasa's ghost
              </span>
             </a>
             :
You have forgotten who you are and so have forgotten me. Look inside yourself, Simba. You are more than what you have become. You must take your place in the Circle of Life.
            </p>

          <div class="quote soda sodavote even" id="qt0371358">
           <div class="sodatext">
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000100/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Zazu
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              singing
             </span>
             ]
Nooooobody knows the trouble I've seen. / Nooooobody knows my sorrow.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Oh, Zazu, do lighten up. Sing something with a little *bounce* in it.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000100/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Zazu
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              singing
             </span>
             ]
It's a small world after all...
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
NO! No. *Anything* but that!
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000100/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Zazu
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              singing
             </span>
             ]
I've got a lovely bunch of coconuts. / Dee-dee-dee-dee, / There they are just standing in a row.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000100/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Zazu
              </span>
             </a>
             ,
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              Scar joins in
             </span>
             ]
Big ones, small ones, some as big as your head...
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000100/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Zazu
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              whispering
             </span>
             ]
Oh, I never had to do this with Mufasa.

           <div class="sodatext">
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0754676/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Pumbaa
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              about "Hakuna Matata"
             </span>
             ]
It's our motto.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
What's a motto?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001447/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Timon
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Nothing. What's a motto with you?
            </p>
            <p>
             [
             <span class="fine">
              laughs
             </span>
             ]
            </p>

             [

             </a>

            </p>

              </span>

            </p>
            <p>

              <span class="character">

              </span>
             </a>
             :

            </p>
            <p>

              <span class="character">

              </span>
             </a>

             </a>

             </a>

ARE YOU TALKING TO ME?
            </p>

          <div class="quote soda sodavote even" id="qt0371434">
           <div class="sodatext">
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000469/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Mufasa
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Everything you see exists together in a delicate balance. As king, you need to understand that balance and respect all the creatures, from the crawling ant to the leaping antelope.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
But, Dad, don't we eat the antelope?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000469/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Mufasa
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Yes, Simba, but let me explain. When we die, our bodies become the grass, and the antelope eat the grass. And so we are all connected in the great Circle of Life.
            </p>

          <div class="quote soda sodavote even" id="qt1003500">
           <div class="sodatext">
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001507/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Banzai
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              In the hyenas' lair, Banzai slouches with claw marks on his rear
             </span>
             ]
Man, that lousy Mufasa... I won't be able to sit for a *week!*
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0191906/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Ed the Hyena
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              laughs, but also tries his best to conceal it from time to time
             </span>
             ]
Eh-hee-hee-hee. Heh-heheheheheheheheheh...
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001507/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Banzai
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              Glares at Ed and bares his teeth with impatience
             </span>
             ]
It's not funny, Ed.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0191906/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Ed the Hyena
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              Cups his paws over his mouth then bursts into hysterical laughter, spitting as his tongue lofts out of his mouth
             </span>
             ]
BA-HA-HA-HAAAA! HA-AH-AH-AH-AH!
            </p>
            <p>
             [
             <span class="fine">
              Inhales deeply
             </span>
             ]
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001507/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Banzai
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Hey, shut up!
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0191906/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Ed the Hyena
              </span>
             </a>
             :
AH-HA-HO! HO-HO-HO-HO!
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001507/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Banzai
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              Bares his teeth
             </span>
             ]
Grrrrrr...
            </p>
            <p>
             [
             <span class="fine">
              as Ed continues to laugh, Banzai barks and pounces on Ed, abruptly ending his laughing. The two commence a brief fight
             </span>
             ]
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000155/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Shenzi
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              Rolls her eyes and turns to the two yelping and rolling atop each other aggressively
             </span>
             ]
Will you knock it off?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001507/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Banzai
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              ed appears to be chewing on Banzai's leg; Banzai sits up
             </span>
             ]
Well, he started it!
            </p>
            <p>
             [
             <span class="fine">
              It is now obvious that Ed is chewing his own leg repeatedly
             </span>
             ]
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000155/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Shenzi
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Look at you guys! No wonder we're dangling at the bottom of the food chain!
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001507/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Banzai
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              a string of drool dangles from his chin
             </span>
             ]
Man, I hate dangling...
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000155/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Shenzi
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              Scoffs
             </span>
             ]
Yeah? You know, if it weren't for those lions, we'd be *runnin'* the joint.
            </p>
            <p>
             [
             <span class="fine">
              Ed nods idiotically
             </span>
             ]
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001507/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Banzai
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Man, I *hate* lions!
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000155/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Shenzi
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              Grumbles
             </span>
             ]
So pushy...
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001507/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Banzai
              </span>
             </a>
             :
And hairy...
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000155/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Shenzi
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              Smiles
             </span>
             ]
Stinky...
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001507/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Banzai
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              Grins
             </span>
             ]
And man are they...
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001507/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Banzai
              </span>
             </a>
             ,
             <a href="/name/nm0000155/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Shenzi
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              Elongated use of the 'u'
             </span>
             ]
U-GLY!
            </p>
            <p>
             [
             <span class="fine">
              both laugh hysterically
             </span>
             ]
            </p>

          <div class="quote soda sodavote even" id="qt0371377">
           <div class="sodatext">
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000100/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Zazu
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Checking in with the morning report.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000469/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Mufasa
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Fire away.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000100/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Zazu
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Well the buzz from the bees is that the leopards are in a bit of a spot. And the baboons are going ape over this. Of course, the giraffes are acting like they're above it all... The tick birds are pecking on the elephants. I told the elephants to forget it, but they can't. The cheetahs are hard up, but I always say, cheetahs never prosper...
            </p>

          <div class="quote soda sodavote odd" id="qt0371451">
           <div class="sodatext">
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              after forcing Simba to the edge of a cliff while a fire burns below
             </span>
             ]
Now this looks familiar. Where have I seen this before? Hm, let me think. Oh, yes, I remember! This is just the way your father looked before he died.
            </p>
            <p>
             [
             <span class="fine">
              He claws Simba's paws the same way he did to Mufasa
             </span>
             ]
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
And here's 'my' little secret...
            </p>
            <p>
             [
             <span class="fine">
              whispering
             </span>
             ]
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
I killed Mufasa!
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              In a flashback
             </span>
             ]
Nooooo!
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000111/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Adult Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              leaps back up and pounces on him
             </span>
             ]
Nooo! Murderer!
            </p>

          <div class="quote soda sodavote even" id="qt1936173">
           <div class="sodatext">
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0347039/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Rafiki
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Look down there.
            </p>
            <p>
             [
             <span class="fine">
              Slowly Simba walks to the edge of the watering hole and peers inside. His reflection stares back at him
             </span>
             ]
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000111/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Adult Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
That's not my father. That's just my reflection.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0347039/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Rafiki
              </span>
             </a>
             :
No. Look harder.
            </p>
            <p>
             [
             <span class="fine">
              Rafiki touches the water which causes waves that change Simba's reflection into Mufasa
             </span>
             ]
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0347039/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Rafiki
              </span>
             </a>
             :
You see? He lives in you.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000469/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Mufasa's Ghost
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              From above
             </span>
             ]
Simba.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000111/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Adult Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Father?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000469/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Mufasa's Ghost
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              He appears in the sky as a group of stars
             </span>
             ]
Simba, you have forgotten me.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000111/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Adult Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
No. How could I?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000469/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Mufasa's Ghost
              </span>
             </a>
             :
You have forgotten who you are and so have forgotten me. Look inside yourself Simba. You are more than what you have become. You must take your place in the Circle of life.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000111/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Adult Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
How can I go back? I'm not who I used to be.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000469/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Mufasa's Ghost
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              Now fully formed in the sky
             </span>
             ]
Remember who you are. You are my son and the one true king. Remember who you are.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000111/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Adult Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              Mufasa's ghost begins to disappear
             </span>
             ]
No! Please! Don't leave me!
            </p>

             <a href="/name/nm0000469/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">

             </a>
             :

            </p>

            </p>

             <a href="/name/nm0000469/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">

              </span>
             </a>
             :
Remember.

             <a href="/name/nm0000111/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">

             :

              </span>
             </a>
             :

              Nala's mother, Sarafina is giving Nala a bath
             </span>
             ]
Hey, Nala.
            </p>

             <a href="/name/nm0129295/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Nala
              </span>
             </a>

               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :

            </p>

             <a href="/name/nm0129295/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Nala
              </span>
             </a>

            </p>

              </span>
             </a>

            </p>

             [
             <span class="fine">
              grabs Simba and starts licking him
             </span>

              </span>
             </a>

            </p>

             [
             <span class="fine">
              Sarabi smiles
             </span>

            </p>

              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>

            </p>

               Young Nala
              </span>
             </a>

              </span>
             </a>

              </span>
             </a>

Well...
            </p>

Please!

Sarabiiiii!
            </p>

             [
             <span class="fine">
              echoes and reechoes; we soon see Sarabi walking through the pack of hyenas, trying to snap at her; Simba looks on as Sarabi approaches
             </span>
             ]
            </p>

             <a href="/name/nm0801672/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">

              </span>
             </a>

            </p>

             <a href="/name/nm0801672/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">

              </span>
             </a>

            </p>

             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
No! You're just not looking hard enough.
            </p>

              </span>
             </a>
             :
It's over. There is nothing left. We have only one choice. We *must* leave Pride Rock.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
We're not going anywhere!
            </p>

              <span class="character">
               Sarabi
              </span>
             </a>

Then you have sentenced us to death!
            </p>

             </a>

            </p>

              <span class="character">

            </p>

             </a>

I'm the king! I can do whatever I want!
            </p>

              <span class="character">
               Sarabi
              </span>
             </a>

If you were half the king Mufasa was, you...
            </p>

              </span>

[
             <span class="fine">
              knocks Sarabi unconscious
             </span>

I'm *ten* times the king Mufasa was!
            </p>

             </span>

          <div class="quote soda sodavote even" id="qt0371400">
           <div class="sodatext">
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Now you wait here. Your father has a *marvelous* surprise for you.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Oooh. What is it?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
If I told you, it wouldn't *be* a surprise, now would it?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
If you tell me, I'll still *act* surprised.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Ho ho ho. You are such a naughty boy!
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Come on, Uncle Scar.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
No, no, no, no, no, no, no. This is just for you and your daddy. You know, a sort of... father-son... thing. Well! I'd better go get him.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
I'll go with you.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
No!
            </p>
            <p>
             [
             <span class="fine">
              regaining composure
             </span>
             ]
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Heh heh heh. No. Just stay on this rock. You wouldn't want to end up in another mess like you did with the hyenas.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
You know about that?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Simba, Simba, everybody knows about that.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Really?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Oh, yes. Lucky Daddy was there to save you, eh? Oh, and just between us, you might want to work on that little roar of yours. Hmm?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Oh, okay. Hey, Uncle Scar, will I like this surprise?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Simba, it's to *die* for!

              <span class="character">
               Adult Simba
              </span>
             </a>

             <a href="/name/nm0347039/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Rafiki
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Can't cut it out. It grow right back!
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000111/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Adult Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Creepy little monkey. Will you stop following me? Who are you?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0347039/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Rafiki
              </span>
             </a>
             :
The question is who are you?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000111/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Adult Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
I thought I knew. Now I'm not so sure.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0347039/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Rafiki
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Well, I know who you are. Ssh, come here. It's a secret.
            </p>
            <p>
             [
             <span class="fine">
              starts singing in Simba's ear
             </span>
             ]
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0347039/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Rafiki
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Asante sana Squash banana, wewe nugu mimi hapana
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000111/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Adult Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Enough already! What is that supposed to mean anyway?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0347039/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Rafiki
              </span>
             </a>
             :
It means you're a baboon and I'm not.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000111/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Adult Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
I think you're a little confused.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0347039/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Rafiki
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Wrong! I'm not the one who's confused. You don't even know who you are!
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000111/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Adult Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Oh and I suppose you know?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0347039/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Rafiki
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Sure do. You're Mufasa's boy!
            </p>
            <p>
             [
             <span class="fine">
              Simba looks at Rafiki
             </span>
             ]
            </p>

             <a href="/name/nm0347039/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Rafiki
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Bye!
            </p>

              <span class="character">
               Adult Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              Rafiki runs off and Simba chases him
             </span>
             ]
Hey wait!
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000111/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Adult Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              Catching up
             </span>
             ]
You knew my father?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0347039/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Rafiki
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Correction. I know you're father.
            </p>

             <a href="/name/nm0000111/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Adult Simba
              </span>
             </a>

I hate to tell you this but he died. A long time ago.

             <a href="/name/nm0347039/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Rafiki
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Nope! wrong again! He's alive and I will show him to you! You follow old Rafiki. He knows the way!

             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Dad?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000469/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Mufasa
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Hmm?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :

            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000469/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Mufasa
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Right.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :

             </a>

              </span>
             </a>

              <span class="character">

              </span>

Ah, you're an outcast! That's great. So are we.

          <div class="quote soda sodavote even" id="qt0371371">
           <div class="sodatext">
            <p>
             [
             <span class="fine">
              singing
             </span>
             ]
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001447/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Timon
              </span>
             </a>
             :
And if he falls / In love tonight / It can be assumed...
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0754676/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Pumbaa
              </span>
             </a>
             :
His carefree days / With us are history.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001447/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Timon
              </span>
             </a>
             ,
             <a href="/name/nm0754676/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Pumbaa
              </span>
             </a>
             :
In short, our pal / Is doomed!
            </p>

           <div class="sodatext">
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000469/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Mufasa
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Don't turn your back on me, Scar!
            </p>

              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :

            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000469/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Mufasa
              </span>
             </a>
             :

             <span class="fine">
              roars, runs to stand before him
             </span>
             ]
Is that a challenge?
            </p>

               Scar
              </span>
             </a>

            </p>

             [
             <span class="fine">
              Nala does so. Simba leaps at Nala again. They tumble down a hill and Nala ends up on top of Simba again
             </span>
             ]
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0129295/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Nala
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Pinned ya again!
            </p>
           </div>

              </span>

             </a>

Wow!

Shhhh! Zazu.

              </span>
             </a>

Right. So how are we going to ditch the dodo?
            </p>

             [
             <span class="fine">

             </span>
             ]

              </span>

Just look at you two. Little seeds of romance blossoming in the savannah. Your parents will be *thrilled*, what with your being betrothed and all.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Be-what?
            </p>

             <a href="/name/nm0000100/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">

              </span>
             </a>

Betrothed. Intended. Affianced.
            </p>

             <a href="/name/nm0129295/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Nala
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Meaning...?
            </p>

             <a href="/name/nm0000100/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Zazu
              </span>
             </a>
             :
One day, you two are going to be married.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Yuck.
            </p>

             <a href="/name/nm0129295/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">

              </span>
             </a>

Ewww.
            </p>

             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>

            </p>

               Young Nala
              </span>
             </a>

Yeah. It'd be so weird.

              </span>
             </a>

Well, sorry to bust the old bubble, but you two turtledoves have no choice. It's a tradition going back generations.
            </p>

              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>

Well, when I'm king, that'll be the first thing to go.

              <span class="character">

              </span>
             </a>

              </span>
             </a>

              </span>
             </a>

Hmmm... Nice try, but only the king can do that.

              <span class="character">

              </span>
             </a>

Well, he's the future king.

              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>

Yeah. So you have to do what I tell you.

              <span class="character">
               Zazu
              </span>
             </a>
             :

            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
So, your father showed you the whole kingdom, did he?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Everything.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
He didn't show you what's beyond that rise at the northern border?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Well, no. He said I can't go there.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
And he's absolutely right! It's far too dangerous. Only the bravest lions go there.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Well, I'm brave. What's out there?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
No, I'm sorry, Simba, I just *can't* tell you.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Why not?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Simba, Simba, I'm only looking out for the well-being of my favorite nephew.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Yeah, right. I'm your only nephew.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
All the more reason for me to be protective. An elephant graveyard is no place for a young prince.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
An elephant what? Whoa!
            </p>

             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>

Oops! Oh, dear, I've said too much! Well, I suppose you'd have found out sooner or later, you being so clever and all. Just promise me you'll never visit that dreadful place!
            </p>

             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">

              </span>
             </a>

            </p>

               Adult Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :

            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
But, Simba, I... am... family. It's the hyenas who are the real enemy. It was their fault. It was their idea!
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000111/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Adult Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Why should I believe you? Everything you ever told me was a lie.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
What are you going to do? You wouldn't kill your *old* uncle...?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000111/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Adult Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
No, Scar. I'm not like you.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Oh, Simba, thank you. You are truly noble. I'll make it up to you, I promise. How can I, ah, prove myself to you? Tell me anything, anything.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000111/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Adult Simba
              </span>
             </a>

Run. Run away, Scar. And never return.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">

             </a>

            </p>

             [
             <span class="fine">

             </span>

             </a>

your Majesty!

             <span class="fine">

              </span>
             </a>
             :
Aaah!

Wrong! When the world turns its back on you, you turn your back on the world.
            </p>

            <p>

              </span>
             </a>

          <div class="quote soda sodavote even" id="qt0371378">
           <div class="sodatext">
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000469/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Mufasa
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Look, Simba. Everything the light touches is our kingdom.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Wow.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000469/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Mufasa
              </span>
             </a>
             :
A king's time as ruler rises and falls like the sun. One day, Simba, the sun will set on my time here, and will rise with you as the new king.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
And this'll all be mine?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000469/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Mufasa
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Everything.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Everything the light touches...
            </p>

          <div class="quote soda sodavote even" id="qt0371402">
           <div class="sodatext">
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Mufasa's death was a terrible tragedy; but to lose Simba, who had barely begun to live... For me it is a deep personal loss. So it is with a heavy heart that I assume the throne. Yet, out of the ashes of this tragedy, we shall rise to greet the dawning of a new era... in which lion and hyena come together, in a great and glorious future!
            </p>
           </div>

            </p>

             <a href="/name/nm0754676/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">

              </span>
             </a>
             :

            </p>

             <a href="/name/nm0001447/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Timon
              </span>
             </a>

            </p>

             <a href="/name/nm0754676/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Pumbaa
              </span>
             </a>

            </p>

              <span class="character">

             </a>
             :

            </p>

              <span class="character">
               Pumbaa
              </span>
             </a>
             :

            </p>

             <a href="/name/nm0001447/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">

              </span>
             </a>
             :
A - huh! That's the stupidest thing I ever heard. Maybe he'll b-... Hey, I got it! What if he's on our side? You know, having a lion around might not be such a bad idea.

             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">

              singing
             </span>

I know that your powers of retention / Are as wet as a warthog's backside / But thick as you are, / Pay attention! / My words are a matter of pride / It's clear from vacant expressions / The lights are not all on upstairs / But we're talking kings and successions / Even *you* can't be caught unawares!

          <div class="quote soda sodavote even" id="qt0995281">
           <div class="sodatext">
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              singing
             </span>
             ]
Of course, / Quid pro quo, / You're expected / To take certain duties on board / The future is littered with prizes / And though I'm the main addressee / The point that I must emphasize is...
            </p>
            <p>
             [
             <span class="fine">
              Leaps in front of a hyena
             </span>
             ]
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
YOU WON'T GET A SNIFF WITHOUT ME!
            </p>
            <p>
             [
             <span class="fine">
              hyena falls into a volcano
             </span>
             ]

          <div class="quote soda sodavote odd" id="qt1054568">
           <div class="sodatext">

             <a href="/name/nm0801672/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">

              </span>
             </a>

              </span>
             </a>

          <div class="quote soda sodavote even" id="qt2214903">
           <div class="sodatext">
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000469/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Mufasa
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Simba, I'm very disappointed in you!
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
I know.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000469/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Mufasa
              </span>
             </a>
             :
You could have been killed. You deliberatly disobeyed me and what's worse, you put Nala in danger!
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
I was just trying to be brave like you.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000469/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Mufasa
              </span>
             </a>
             :
I'm only brave when I *have* to be. Simba, being brave doesn't mean you go looking for trouble.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
But you're not scared of anything.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000469/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Mufasa
              </span>
             </a>
             :
I was today.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
You were?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000469/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Mufasa
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Yes. I thought I might lose you.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Oh. I guess even kings get scared, huh?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000469/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Mufasa
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Mm-hmm
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
But you know what?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000469/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Mufasa
              </span>
             </a>
             :
What?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
I think those hyenas were even scarder
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000469/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Mufasa
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Cause nobody messes with your dad! Come here you!
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              Mufasa grabs Simba and gives him a noogie
             </span>
             ]
Oh no, no! Aah!
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              Simba squirms away and chases his father and tackles him
             </span>
             ]
Come here. Got ya!
            </p>
            <p>
             [
             <span class="fine">
              They roll in the grass laughing
             </span>
             ]
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Dad?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000469/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Mufasa
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Hmm?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
We're pals right?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000469/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Mufasa
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Right.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
And we'll always be together right?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000469/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Mufasa
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Simba, let me tell you something that *my* father told me. Look at the stars. The great kings of the past look down on us from those stars.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001795/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Young Simba
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Really?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000469/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Mufasa
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Yes. So whenever you feel alone just remember that those kings will always be there to guide you. And so will I.
            </p>

          <div class="quote soda sodavote odd" id="qt0371399">
           <div class="sodatext">
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001507/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Banzai
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Yeah, be prepared! We'll be prepared... for what?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
For the death of the king!
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001507/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Banzai
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Why? Is he sick?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
No, fool, we're going to kill him. And Simba, too.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000155/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Shenzi
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Hey, great idea! Who needs a king?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001507/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Banzai
              </span>
             </a>
             ,
             <a href="/name/nm0000155/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Shenzi
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              singing and dancing around Ed
             </span>
             ]
No king, no king, la la la la la la...
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Idiots! There will *be* a king!
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001507/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Banzai
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Hey, but you said that...
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
*I* will be king. Stick with me, and you'll never go hungry again!
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001507/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Banzai
              </span>
             </a>
             ,
             <a href="/name/nm0000155/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Shenzi
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Yeah, all right! Long live the king!
            </p>
            <p>
             [
             <span class="fine">
              other hyenas join in
             </span>
             ]
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001507/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Banzai
              </span>
             </a>
             ,
             <a href="/name/nm0000155/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Shenzi
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Long live the king! Long live the king!
            </p>

            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0446702/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Nala
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Have you guys seen Simba?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001447/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Timon
              </span>
             </a>
             :
I thought he was with you.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0446702/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Nala
              </span>
             </a>
             :
He was but now I can't find him. Where is he?
            </p>
            <p>
             [
             <span class="fine">
              We hear Rafiki's laugh. He's sitting in a tree above them
             </span>
             ]
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0347039/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Rafiki
              </span>
             </a>
             :
You won't find him here. The king... has returned.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0446702/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Nala
              </span>
             </a>
             :
I can't believe it. He's gone back!
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001447/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Timon
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Gone back? What do you mean?
            </p>
            <p>
             [
             <span class="fine">
              He looks to the tree. Rafiki has disappeared
             </span>
             ]
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001447/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Timon
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Hey! What's going on here? Who's the monkey?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0446702/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Nala
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Simba's gone back to challenge Scar.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001447/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Timon
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Who?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0446702/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Nala
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Scar.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0754676/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Pumbaa
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Who's got a scar?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0446702/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Nala
              </span>
             </a>
             :
No, no, no. It's his uncle.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0001447/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Timon
              </span>
             </a>
             :

            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0446702/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Nala
              </span>
             </a>

          <div class="quote soda sodavote even" id="qt1640480">
           <div class="sodatext">
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000100/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Zazu
              </span>
             </a>
             :
As the king's brother *you* should have been first in line.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000469/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Mufasa
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Well I was first in line. Until the little hairball was born.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000469/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Mufasa
              </span>
             </a>
             :
That hairball is my son and you're future king.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              Begins walking away
             </span>
             ]
Oh, I shall practice my curtsey
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000469/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Mufasa
              </span>
             </a>
             :

            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Oh, no Mufasa. Perhaps *you* shouldn't turn your back on *me*
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000469/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Mufasa
              </span>
             </a>
             :
[
             <span class="fine">
              Roars angrily and runs in front of Scar's path
             </span>
             ]
Is that a challenge?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Temper temper. I wouldn't dream of challenging you.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000100/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Zazu
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Pity. Why not?
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="/name/nm0000460/?ref_=tt_trv_qu">
              <span class="character">
               Scar
              </span>
             </a>
             :
Well as far as brains go I got the lion's share but when it comes to brute strength. I'm afraid I'm at the shallow end of the gene pool
            </p>
           </div>
